Movie News

Lianhua's First Sound Film "Waves Washing Sand" to be Released Soon Lianhua's first film. Lianhua Company has been established for several years, and the films it has produced have been welcomed by audiences at home and abroad. However, all of its products have always been silent films with配击. Recently, in order to keep up with the trend, it has specialized in producing dialogue sound films. After a year of preparation, it is finally being released. "Waves Washing Sand" is its first product. Of course, this Lianhua's first sound film, which has been called for a thousand times, is indeed worth paying attention to.

Opening up new themes. Chinese film themes are obviously becoming increasingly constrained due to various influences. Under this circumstance, "Waves Washing Sand" can be said to be a film that opens up new themes.

The front of the script reads:

"A kind person will commit a crime in an accidental unfortunate encounter; a law-abiding detective is forever pursuing the criminals they want to arrest. When these two people stand on the same line of life, they will abandon their hostility and become the highest form of friendship; but once they encounter a conflict of interest and the agitation of human desires, they will immediately restore their hostility. This kind of tragedy is forever produced between people."

Just from reading those few preface sentences, we can know that this is a new type of影剧.

The sad and tragic poem "Waves Washing Sand" is extremely poetic. After watching this film, we seem to be immersed in the realm of poetry, but this poem is not a fantasy, but a very practical and tragic poem.

Human blood records. Human history is written in blood, but there is originally no hatred between people, only because they need to survive, cannot understand each other, and forever plunder, kill, and wage war against each other. This "Waves Washing Sand" can be said to be a microcosm of the human world, and can also be said to be a record of human blood.

Lai Fu Bailaimei and Ge Lulixiya co-star in "Business Warfare Inside Story"

Human Shanghai Reflects

Emphasizing psychological depiction. "Waves Washing Sand" not only has a transcendent meaning in its theme, but also has a special success in its depiction. As a whole, it starts from the psychology of human beings and writes a tragedy that contains infinite philosophical meaning, which can make every viewer have a personal spiritual touch.

Exterior scenes taken from Qingdao. A quarter of the entire film is set against the background of a beach and a lonely island, which was taken from Qingdao. The sea and sky are the same color, the scenery is natural, and the raging waves are majestic. Dao Jue "The harvest of "Waves Washing Sand" in terms of exterior scenery can be said to be extremely satisfactory.

Interior scenes can be arranged. 布景师, Xu Ke, is a new and excellent talent. The setting of "Little Angel" was made by him. This is his second collaboration with the film director Wu Yonggang. Xu Jun's setting, simple money rules, has a unique style. The excellent achievement of the setting in this "Waves Washing Sand" is enough to放 one outstanding color in Chinese film settings.

Photography and sound recording are excellent. The photography of "Waves Washing Sand" is handled by photographers Hong Weilie and Zhou Damin. They have achieved amazing success in配光. The sound recording is by Kuang Zan. Because this is Lianhua's first sound film, they are meticulous and naturally have excellent results. In the past and present domestic sound films, the light is clear and soft, and the sound is clear and loud. In terms of vision and hearing, this can be considered a relatively satisfactory sound film.

Jin Yan and Zhang Zhizhi. "Waves Washing Sand" is not only Lianhua's first sound film, but also Jin Yan's first sound masterpiece in Lianhua. Watching Jin Yan's amazing acting skills in this film, it is not an exaggeration to say that it is the greatest success he has seen in the past three years. And Zhang Zhizhi has taken a step further on the ladder in "Goddess". Partnering with Jin Yan in this play can be called a perfect combination.

Director Wu Yonggang. The director of this film is Wu Yonggang. Wu Yonggang became famous with the film "Goddess", and then made the film "Little Angel", which was especially praised by those who are enthusiastic about film education. "Waves Washing Sand" is his third work, and the good results are naturally expected.

This film will be released soon. As it has been discussed with film people across the country, this film has been scheduled to be released in Shanghai and other parts of the country in the coming days

Regarding Understanding Domestically Produced Airplanes

— Meng

I was just delighted by the new record of trade surpluses for external trade in December of last year and January of this year! However, the Jianghai Customs announced that Shanghai's external trade exports decreased and imports increased in February, reversing to a deficit, with a deficit amount of 1,777,391 yuan. In that case, what is the use of the December surplus of 1,080,000 yuan and the January surplus of 1,392,073 yuan in the 25th year of the Republic? The people of the nation should redouble their efforts to promote and use domestic goods, and understand them more fully, so that it will be possible to achieve monthly trade surpluses. Therefore, I find it extremely commendable that the Chinese Naval Aircraft Manufacturing Department has been able to use domestic materials to manufacture a self-made biplane seaplane/amphibious aircraft! According to reports, "This aircraft is intended for flight training, so in addition to the pilot, it can also seat one person. Except for the engine, which was purchased from the United States, all the hardware, enamel, fir, canvas, and all miscellaneous items are domestic products."

We know that saving the nation with domestic goods and saving the nation with aviation are equally important. Recognizing the interest in aviation, it is even more important to recognize the interest in promoting domestic goods. "We have a domestic airplane!" Everyone can clap and cheer, shouting resounding slogans!

Dr. Lü Miannan of Nanjing Successfully Researches and Refines Gasoline

— Shou

Each Ton of Coal Can Refine Ten Gallons; Other Byproducts Are Also Numerous

In the past few decades, all of China's industries have developed extraordinarily, especially the automobile and aviation industries, which have made rapid progress. This is naturally something that we find gratifying. But in everything, we must observe carefully. The growing development of the automobile and aviation industries is, of course, a good phenomenon. But on the other hand, we must consider where the essential commodity used by automobiles and airplanes—gasoline—comes from? Anyone with even a little common sense knows that our country does not produce gasoline. Therefore, the gasoline we currently use is supplied by countries such as England, America, and Russia. In the past, the outflow of gasoline was not so alarming, but since the development of the automobile and airplane industries, the import of gasoline has been staggering. According to past newspaper reports, the annual outflow of gasoline is always several tens of millions of yuan. Even in the year of promoting domestic goods, the amount of gasoline imported is still increasing daily, because cars and airplanes cannot run without gasoline as fuel, and there is no domestic substitute besides relying on foreign goods. So, we have no choice but to use foreign goods with a painful heart!

It is said that the raw material for gasoline is refined from coal. The production of coal is very abundant in our country, especially in Shanxi Province, where coal mines are everywhere. If the Chinese people can refine it, then there will be no shortage of this raw material, coal. Not only can we be self-sufficient, but we may even be able to supply foreign countries! Unfortunately, most people have not paid attention to this point, and foreign gasoline continues to be imported, which is such a heartbreaking thing!

Dr. Lü Miannan, the director of the Chemical Laboratory of the Capital Construction Committee, is a person with a purpose. He has been paying attention to this for several years. After several years of research, he has made considerable achievements in refining gasoline—one might even say a considerable success. The raw material he uses to refine gasoline is bituminous coal. He has refined bituminous coal from various places, and the best is the bituminous coal produced in Leping County, Jiangxi. There are roughly two refining methods: the first is low-temperature distillation, but each ton of coal (1,680 catties) can only refine ten gallons of gasoline, although there are many byproducts, such as coking coal, asphalt, and phenol. The second is light refining: each ton of coal can refine a lot of oil, but there are no byproducts. Comparing the two, low-temperature distillation is more cost-effective, so the first method is still used. He has already refined a considerable amount, and the results are very good.

It is said that when refining gasoline from bituminous coal, there are several separations. The first is called light oil, which is used to make gasoline. The second is called middle oil; the third is called heavy oil. Middle oil and heavy oil cannot be refined into gasoline, but they can be refined into kerosene (i.e., lamp oil) and machine oil. The last is oil residue, which can be made into asphalt and paraffin, and phenol can also be used to make bakelite appliances. So, this kind of oil refining is very cost-effective.

Their refining of gasoline can be considered a success! The second step should naturally be to set up a factory to manufacture it. However, capital is also a problem. The minimum requirement is probably more than one million yuan. They are planning to apply to the Ministry of Industry for a patent at a suitable time! We hope that their plan to set up a factory for manufacturing can be realized soon.

Regarding the refining procedures, due to space limitations, I will report on them when there is an opportunity!

The Necessity of Organizing Children's Domestic Goods Consumption Groups

— Xi

Children's awareness is naive, and their experience is weak. It is easy for them to be taken advantage of in everything. Take the example of children buying things. They are often deceived into buying many foreign goods by unscrupulous merchants who use sweet talk, because children only care about whether the goods look good, and they mostly ignore whether the source of the goods is domestic or foreign. In fact, it is not surprising that they do so. Who in school or at home often points out the differences between domestic and foreign goods? What they hear from adults is only abstract terms such as "use domestic goods" and "don't buy foreign goods." Therefore, in the future, if we want children to truly take the step of not buying foreign goods and using domestic goods, then it is necessary to actively organize children's domestic goods consumption groups.

A children's domestic goods consumption group is a way for children to encourage each other, supervise each other, and take the step of not buying foreign goods and using domestic goods. The group can also elect five or seven members to form a committee, so that everyone can take responsibility for this type of work. As for how not to buy foreign goods? How to use domestic goods? How to distinguish between foreign and domestic goods? How to deal with children who buy foreign goods? How to check what children buy? And other messy and urgent problems, naturally they (the children) will jointly discuss good methods in meetings. Teachers only stand in the position of guidance, instructing children on all common knowledge related to domestic goods and methods of using domestic goods.

In short, if children's domestic goods consumption groups can be organized everywhere, the observation power of children's understanding of domestic and foreign goods can definitely be greatly enhanced, and everyone will definitely be able to develop the habit of using domestic goods. It will definitely be of great benefit to the future of domestic goods. I sincerely hope that the teachers in various places who are responsible for educating children will quickly instruct the children to organize children's domestic goods consumption groups.
